def jagged_hstu_attention(max_seq_len: int, alpha: float, attn_scale: float, q: torch.Tensor, k: torch.Tensor, v: torch.Tensor, seq_offsets: torch.Tensor, *, _launcher=_default_pallas_fori_launcher):
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:89]: num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78]: def jagged_hstu_attention(
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:79]:     max_seq_len: int,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:80]:     alpha: float,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78-130]: ...
    out = getattr(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, '_helion_output_meta_cache_0', None)
    if out is None:
        out = _helion_jagged_hstu_attention._helion_output_meta_cache_0 = torch.empty_like(v, device='meta')
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92]: for tile_b in hl.tile(num_sequences):
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:94]:     # v1's ``jagged_hstu_attn.py:114``). With scalar ``start``,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92-128]: ...
    out = _launcher(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, (1,), seq_offsets, q, out, k, v, torch.tensor([alpha], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(alpha, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), torch.tensor([attn_scale], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(attn_scale, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), _output_indices=[2], _inplace_indices=[], _block_spec_info=[((None,), (None,)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), None, None], _ds_pad_dims=[(1, 0, 8, 7), (2, 0, 8, 7), (3, 0, 8192, 8191), (4, 0, 8192, 8191)], _smem_arg_indices=[0], _scratch_shapes=[((8, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((8, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((32, 8, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((8192, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((8192, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore')], _pipeline_arg_indices=[1, 2, 3, 4])

    return out

def jagged_hstu_attention(max_seq_len: int, alpha: float, attn_scale: float, q: torch.Tensor, k: torch.Tensor, v: torch.Tensor, seq_offsets: torch.Tensor, *, _launcher=_default_pallas_fori_launcher):

    num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78]: def jagged_hstu_attention(

    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:80]:     alpha: float,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78-130]: ...
    out = getattr(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, '_helion_output_meta_cache_0', None)
    if out is None:
        out = _helion_jagged_hstu_attention._helion_output_meta_cache_0 = torch.empty_like(v, device='meta')
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92]: for tile_b in hl.tile(num_sequences):
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:94]:     # v1's ``jagged_hstu_attn.py:114``). With scalar ``start``,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92-128]: ...
    out = _launcher(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, (1,), seq_offsets, q, out, k, v, torch.tensor([alpha], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(alpha, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), torch.tensor([attn_scale], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(attn_scale, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), _output_indices=[2], _inplace_indices=[], _block_spec_info=[((None,), (None,)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), None, None], _ds_pad_dims=[(1, 0, 1024, 1023), (2, 0, 1024, 1023), (3, 0, 128, 127), (4, 0, 128, 127)], _smem_arg_indices=[0], _scratch_shapes=[((1024, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((1024, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((32, 1024, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((128, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((128, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore')], _pipeline_arg_indices=[1, 2, 3, 4])

    return out

    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as

def jagged_hstu_attention(max_seq_len: int, alpha: float, attn_scale: float, q: torch.Tensor, k: torch.Tensor, v: torch.Tensor, seq_offsets: torch.Tensor, *, _launcher=_default_pallas_fori_launcher):
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:89]: num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78]: def jagged_hstu_attention(
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:79]:     max_seq_len: int,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:80]:     alpha: float,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78-130]: ...
    out = getattr(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, '_helion_output_meta_cache_0', None)
    if out is None:
        out = _helion_jagged_hstu_attention._helion_output_meta_cache_0 = torch.empty_like(v, device='meta')
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92]: for tile_b in hl.tile(num_sequences):
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:94]:     # v1's ``jagged_hstu_attn.py:114``). With scalar ``start``,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92-128]: ...
    out = _launcher(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, (1,), seq_offsets, q, out, k, v, torch.tensor([alpha], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(alpha, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), torch.tensor([attn_scale], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(attn_scale, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), _output_indices=[2], _inplace_indices=[], _block_spec_info=[((None,), (None,)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), None, None], _ds_pad_dims=[(1, 0, 8, 7), (2, 0, 8, 7), (3, 0, 1024, 1023), (4, 0, 1024, 1023)], _smem_arg_indices=[0], _scratch_shapes=[((8, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((8, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((32, 8, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((1024, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((1024, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore')], _pipeline_arg_indices=[1, 2, 3, 4])

    return out

    num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78]: def jagged_hstu_attention(
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:79]:     max_seq_len: int,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:80]:     alpha: float,

    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as

    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78]: def jagged_hstu_attention(

    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as

    num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78]: def jagged_hstu_attention(
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:79]:     max_seq_len: int,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:80]:     alpha: float,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78-130]: ...
    out = getattr(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, '_helion_output_meta_cache_0', None)
    if out is None:
        out = _helion_jagged_hstu_attention._helion_output_meta_cache_0 = torch.empty_like(v, device='meta')
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92]: for tile_b in hl.tile(num_sequences):
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:94]:     # v1's ``jagged_hstu_attn.py:114``). With scalar ``start``,

    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as

    num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78]: def jagged_hstu_attention(
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:79]:     max_seq_len: int,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:80]:     alpha: float,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78-130]: ...
    out = getattr(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, '_helion_output_meta_cache_0', None)
    if out is None:
        out = _helion_jagged_hstu_attention._helion_output_meta_cache_0 = torch.empty_like(v, device='meta')
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92]: for tile_b in hl.tile(num_sequences):
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:94]:     # v1's ``jagged_hstu_attn.py:114``). With scalar ``start``,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92-128]: ...
    out = _launcher(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, (1,), seq_offsets, q, out, k, v, torch.tensor([alpha], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(alpha, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), torch.tensor([attn_scale], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(attn_scale, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), _output_indices=[2], _inplace_indices=[], _block_spec_info=[((None,), (None,)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), None, None], _ds_pad_dims=[(1, 0, 8192, 8191), (2, 0, 8192, 8191), (3, 0, 1024, 1023), (4, 0, 1024, 1023)], _smem_arg_indices=[0], _scratch_shapes=[((8192, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((8192, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((32, 8192, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((1024, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((1024, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore')], _pipeline_arg_indices=[1, 2, 3, 4])

def jagged_hstu_attention(max_seq_len: int, alpha: float, attn_scale: float, q: torch.Tensor, k: torch.Tensor, v: torch.Tensor, seq_offsets: torch.Tensor, *, _launcher=_default_pallas_fori_launcher):
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:89]: num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    num_sequences = seq_offsets.size(0) - 1
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78]: def jagged_hstu_attention(
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:79]:     max_seq_len: int,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:80]:     alpha: float,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:78-130]: ...
    out = getattr(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, '_helion_output_meta_cache_0', None)
    if out is None:
        out = _helion_jagged_hstu_attention._helion_output_meta_cache_0 = torch.empty_like(v, device='meta')
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92]: for tile_b in hl.tile(num_sequences):
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:93]:     # ``tile_b.begin`` gives a scalar program index (same idiom as
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:94]:     # v1's ``jagged_hstu_attn.py:114``). With scalar ``start``,
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:92-128]: ...
    out = _launcher(_helion_jagged_hstu_attention, (1,), seq_offsets, q, out, k, v, torch.tensor([alpha], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(alpha, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), torch.tensor([attn_scale], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(attn_scale, float) else torch.int32, device=seq_offsets.device), _output_indices=[2], _inplace_indices=[], _block_spec_info=[((None,), (None,)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), ((None, None, None), (None, None, None)), None, None], _ds_pad_dims=[(1, 0, 256, 255), (2, 0, 256, 255), (3, 0, 8192, 8191), (4, 0, 8192, 8191)], _smem_arg_indices=[0], _scratch_shapes=[((256, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((256, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((32, 256, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((8192, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((8192, 32, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore')], _pipeline_arg_indices=[1, 2, 3, 4])
    # src[jagged_hstu_attn_3.py:130]: return out
    return out
